msg:I recently stayed at the Pagoda Hotel in Shenzhen, and overall, it left me with mixed feelings. The hotel itself is quite nice and modern, and the bed was exceptionally comfortable. The bathroom had a great shower that was a real pleasure to use.

However, my experience was marred by the persistent smell of cigarettes in my room, which was a major disappointment. The room is supposed to be ‚Äúnon-smoking‚Äù but maybe they don‚Äôt enforce this rule. Despite the staff's efforts to mitigate the issue by providing an air purifier and opening the window, the smell lingered, affecting my overall comfort.

Another inconvenience I encountered was that the housekeeping staff entered my room despite the "do not disturb" sign on my door, which was a privacy concern.

While the Pagoda Hotel has many positive aspects, such as its modern amenities and comfortable bedding, the cigarette odor and the housekeeping issue were significant drawbacks during my stay. It's essential for the hotel to address these issues to ensure a more pleasant experience for future guests.

msg:geographical location

It is close to Haiya Colorful City and only a few minutes' walk away (I found out after taking a taxi) that there are KFC, Naixue, Starbucks and 711 downstairs of the hotel, which is very convenient.
It's not far from Happy Harbor. The deluxe room we stayed in on the first night could see the Ferris wheel.
Although it is not very close to the center, it is quite convenient overall.

overall environment

There is nothing to fault at this price. The overall equipment is very new and the room is very clean. With children, I like hotels with a newer environment and good hygiene. The deluxe room is quite large, the electric toilet is also very good, and the small refrigerator is also very cute. Voice control is very convenient. The next day I originally planned to pay the price difference to upgrade to a parent-child room, but the front desk was very nice. After understanding the situation, they upgraded me directly and gave me a tour of both rooms. The whole place is very clean, and there are children's supplies and nightgowns, which is very nice.

meals

Although I personally don't feel that the variety of breakfast is particularly rich, it has everything that should be included. It also changes in two days, which is not to say that it is static. I particularly recommend the raw porridge and rice rolls, which are really good. Hotels of this level usually charge extra for breakfast, but Ctrip and hotel packages include breakfast, so there is nothing to fault. There are also many choices for drinks.

Serve

There's really not much else to say. It's great. They are very patient and kind. When the children cry, everyone comforts them. They are also very caring and considerate. I will definitely stay here again just because of this service.

I originally wanted to stay for two more days this time, but my child kept insisting on going to the big room in the Duck, so I had to change hotels. However, if I come to Bao'an District next time, it will still be my first choice. It would be nice if the parent-child rooms could be more abundant.
